### [119] [Layer Equivalence Is Not a Property of Layers Alone: How You Test Redundancy Changes What You Find](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16234)
*Gabriel Garcia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了Transformer压缩中“替换”与“交换”评估协议的显著差异，指出两者在剪枝决策中并不等价，并建议在剪枝前同时评估这两种swap-KL指标以确保安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前研究在评估Transformer层压缩的等效性时，往往混淆了“替换（Replacement，能否替代）”和“交换（Interchange，能否对易）”这两个概念。作者旨在揭示这两种协议之间的分歧，以及这种差异如何导致剪枝安全性的评估出现巨大偏差。

Method: 通过在不同的Transformer检查点（Pythia 410M/1.4B、Qwen3-8B、Llama-3.1-8B）上进行实证测量，比较“替换”和“交换”两种评估协议在模型剪枝中的表现。该方法仅需无标签的前向传播，即可计算swap-KL得分。

Result: 研究发现：1. 在Pythia训练轨迹中，随着模型收敛，两种协议的差距会不断扩大；2. 不同架构对协议的选择极其敏感，例如Qwen3-8B中交换法比替换法剪枝更安全，而Llama-3.1-8B中两者成本相近；3. 指标差异与移除结果并非一一对应。

Conclusion: 研究强调，在评估Transformer层剪枝的等效性时，不能仅依赖单一指标。研究者应当在进行层删除或合并前，同时计算“替换（Replacement）”和“交换（Interchange）”两种swap-KL指标，因为协议之间的差异会显著影响剪枝策略的安全性和有效性。

Abstract: When researchers ask whether two transformer layers are "equivalent" for compression, they often conflate distinct tests. Replacement asks whether one layer's map can substitute for another's in place; interchange asks whether two layers approximately commute when their positions are swapped. Both are output-grounded swap-KL probes, but they need not agree: on pretrained transformers the protocol gap can change which layers look safe to prune by several-fold under the same evaluator, especially when replacement distances are high.
  We measure both protocols across checkpoints and architectures. On a Pythia training trajectory (410M and 1.4B), the replacement-interchange gap grows from initialization to convergence. Under one matched WikiText-2 contract at 8B scale, Qwen3-8B enters a divergent regime: interchange-guided removal is several-fold safer than replacement-guided at the same layer budgets, while Llama-3.1-8B ties the two protocols for pruning cost even though interchange KL is lower, showing metric gaps need not map one-to-one to removal. Before layer removal or merging, score both swap-KLs on the target checkpoint; the diagnostic requires only unlabeled forward passes.

</details>


### [120] [IO-SVD: Input-Output Whitened SVD for Adaptive-Rank LLM Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15626)
*Ali Abbasi,Chayne Thrash,Haoran Qin,Hamed Pirsiavash,Soheil Kolouri*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: IO-SVD是一种创新的后训练压缩框架，通过双侧白化空间构建、基于KL散度的智能秩分配以及损失感知的混合量化策略，显著提升了大型模型在压缩后的性能保留能力与推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）的存储和计算成本高昂，限制了其在资源受限和延迟敏感场景下的部署。传统的基于SVD的压缩方法往往受限于输入侧白化、均匀秩分配及缺乏损失感知的启发式策略，导致在高压缩比下模型性能严重下降。因此，研究人员旨在寻求一种能更好保持模型质量的后训练压缩方法。

Method: 1. 提出IO-SVD方法，通过构建基于KL散度的双侧（输入输出）白化空间，更准确地捕捉权重的重要性；2. 引入一种高效的异构秩分配策略，利用一阶校准损失估计来修剪不敏感的奇异分量；3. 改进了SVD与量化的混合压缩策略，通过损失感知重映射技术，精准选择低秩因子进行8-bit量化。

Result: 在多种LLM和VLM模型上的实验表明，IO-SVD能够在极小性能损失的前提下，显著减小模型体积，并提供实用的推理加速效果。

Conclusion: IO-SVD通过结合双侧白化、基于KL散度的异构秩分配以及损失感知量化重映射，成功克服了现有SVD压缩方法在模型精度保持与压缩率之间的瓶颈，为资源受限环境下的LLM部署提供了一种高效、硬件无关的解决方案。

Abstract: Large language models deliver strong performance across language and reasoning tasks, but their storage and compute costs remain major barriers to deployment in resource-constrained and latency-sensitive settings. SVD-based post-training compression offers a hardware-agnostic way to reduce model size and improve inference efficiency through low-rank factorization. However, existing methods often rely on input-only whitening spaces, homogeneous rank allocation, or loss-agnostic allocation heuristics, limiting their ability to preserve model quality under aggressive compression. We propose Input-Output Whitened SVD (IO-SVD), a post-training compression method that forms a KL-aware double-sided whitening space for model weights. Using a second-order expansion of the KL loss over the top-K token probabilities, IO-SVD constructs an output-side metric that captures predictive sensitivity, while input whitening captures activation statistics. We further introduce an efficient heterogeneous rank-allocation strategy that scores whitened singular components using first-order calibration loss estimates and prunes the least sensitive components under a global budget. Inspired by prior work that combines SVD truncation with quantization, we improve hybrid SVD-quantization compression through loss-aware remapping, which selects low-rank factor rows for 8-bit quantization based on the predicted loss change incurred by quantizing them. Extensive experiments across diverse LLM and VLM families, and inference-time analysis shows that IO-SVD compresses LLMs with minimal performance degradation while delivering practical inference speedups. Code is available at https://github.com/mint-vu/IO-SVD.git

</details>


### [121] [$f$-Trajectory Balance: A Loss Family for Tuning GFlowNets, Generative Models, and LLMs with Off- and On-Policy Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15417)
*Jake Fawkes,Jason Hartford*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文将生成模型训练中常用的均方误差损失推广至整个f-散度家族，提出了一类既能在离策略（off-policy）数据下高效训练，又能保持策略内（on-policy）梯度一致性及特定f-散度特性的新型替代损失函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型训练（如GFlowNets和变分推断）中常用的均方误差（MSE）损失函数虽然有效，但仅局限于特定的距离度量。研究者希望将这种特性扩展到更广泛的f-散度家族，以利用不同f-散度（如更具模态覆盖能力）的特性，并解决离策略学习中的目标一致性问题。

Method: 提出了一个基于f-散度的生成模型训练框架。通过证明目标对数概率与模型对数概率之间的平移不变损失函数与f-散度在策略内（on-policy）梯度上的等价性，构造出了一类新的替代损失函数。该方法允许在离策略数据上进行训练，同时确保其全局极小值与目标f-散度一致。

Result: 在合成数据、分子发现（SynFlowNets）及大语言模型（LLM）异步微调等任务中验证了该方法的有效性。结果表明，新设计的损失函数在离策略设置下能够成功优化生成模型，并保留了对应f-散度的特定性质（如改进的模态覆盖效果）。

Conclusion: 该研究通过建立平移不变损失函数与f-散度之间的对应关系，为生成模型提供了一类稳健的、适用于离策略（off-policy）训练的替代损失函数。这些损失函数不仅继承了f-散度的特性（如模态覆盖能力），还保持了与策略内（on-policy）梯度的一致性，在分子发现和LLM微调等任务中展现了优越的性能。

Abstract: In GFlowNets and variational inference, it has been shown that the mean square error between target and model log probabilities is an effective, low variance, surrogate loss for training generative models.
  This loss has the property that when evaluated \emph{on-policy} its gradients correspond to those of the KL divergence, while \emph{off-policy} it remains a valid loss with the same global minimizer. In this work, we demonstrate that this construction can be extended to the whole family of $f$-divergences, leading to a family of losses whose on-policy gradients are that of the corresponding $f$-divergence, but retain the same global minimizer off-policy. Specifically, we show that the on-policy gradients lead to a one to one correspondence between translation invariant loss functions on the target and model log probabilities, and $f$-divergences. This equivalence allows us to design new surrogate loss functions for tuning a wide class of generative models that inherit the properties of the corresponding $f$-divergence, such as being more mode covering, whilst being applicable to off-policy data. We apply our losses on a range of tasks, including classic synthetic examples, SynFlowNets for molecule discovery, and asynchronous large language model (LLM) tuning, demonstrating that our models retain their predicted properties on- and off-policy in a wide class of generative models.

</details>


### [122] [Sharp Spectral Thresholds for Logit Fixed Points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15651)
*Tongxi Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过推导出一个更精确、与维度无关的数学判据，修正了关于Softmax反馈系统稳定性的经典认识，在更广泛的参数范围内保证了系统的全局可预测性，并明确了系统发生相变的临界点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Softmax反馈系统是多种领域（如强化学习、博弈论等）的核心机制，但现有的经典稳定性理论过于保守，仅在强随机化情形下有效，无法准确识别系统何时真正发生稳定性丧失（分岔）的质变，导致模型在接近相变区域时缺乏有效的理论保障。

Method: 研究通过数学证明方法，针对有限维仿射Logit系统，推导并建立了一个新的稳定性判据（即 β\|ΠWΠ\|_{\mathcal T\to\mathcal T}<2）。研究对比了经典理论基于单元尺度响应的保守界限，通过分析算子范数，界定了系统从稳定到不稳定的真实相变临界点。

Result: 研究证明了现有的稳定性条件忽略了一个完整的稳定区域。通过引入新的阈值条件，论文成功弥补了预分岔区域的理论空白，在奖励响应与系统全局可预测性之间建立起更广泛的稳定边界，并精确识别了系统发生相变的临界状态。

Conclusion: 该研究推导出了仿射Logit反馈系统的尖锐且与维度无关的欧几里得稳定性阈值。这一发现修正了经典理论中过于保守的限制，不仅扩展了对奖励响应系统全局稳定性的保证范围，还精准定位了系统发生相变的临界点，为理解复杂反馈系统的动态行为提供了更深入的理论框架。

Abstract: Softmax feedback systems are a common mathematical core of entropy-regularized reinforcement learning, logit game dynamics, population choice, and mean-field variational updates. Their central stability question is simple: when does a self-reinforcing softmax system produce a unique and globally predictable outcome? Classical theory gives a conservative answer. By treating softmax as a unit-scale response, it certifies stability only in a strongly randomized regime.
  We prove that the classical approach misses an entire stable regime and does not identify the point at which the qualitative change truly occurs. For finite-dimensional affine logit systems, the sharp dimension-free Euclidean threshold is $$β\|ΠWΠ\|_{\mathcal T\to\mathcal T}<2,$$ rather than the previously used condition, which certifies stability only while the softmax system remains safely over-regularized. Our theorem fills the previously missing pre-bifurcation regime, extending stability guarantees for affine softmax feedback systems to reward-responsive yet globally predictable systems. It enlarges the certified stability boundary for these systems and identifies where the model genuinely undergoes a phase transition.

</details>


### [123] [On the Power of Adaptivity for $\varepsilon$-Best Arm Identification in Linear Bandits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15663)
*Arnab Maiti,Yunbei Xu,Kevin Jamieson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了线性Bandit问题中的$\varepsilon$-最佳臂识别，界定了非自适应算法的样本复杂度下界，并证明了虽然在许多自然结构下自适应仅有对数级优势，但对于特定构造的行动集，自适应策略能带来多项式级别的样本复杂度降低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线性Bandit问题中，对于$\varepsilon$-最佳臂识别，探究如何在满足给定置信度条件下，通过最少的采样次数准确识别出近似最优的动作，并分析自适应采样相比于非自适应采样在不同结构下的性能差异。

Method: 1. 提出了非自适应固定设计方法，并推导了其匹配的下界；
2. 探讨了在不同行动集结构（如超立方体、$\ell_2$球等）下，自适应采样相对于非自适应采样带来的改进程度；
3. 设计了一种针对$\ell_2$范数估计的自适应子程序，并以此构造了使自适应具有多项式优势的特定行动集。

Result: 1. 非自适应固定设计方法的样本复杂度为$\mathcal{O}\left(\frac{d\log(1/\delta)}{\varepsilon^2}+\frac{w(\mathcal{X})^2}{\varepsilon^2}\right)$；
2. 对于超立方体、$\ell_2$球等自然行动集，自适应仅带来对数级的改进；
3. 首次构造了存在多项式级自适应优势的行动集，并给出了相应的算法。

Conclusion: 本文建立了线性Bandit中$\varepsilon$-最佳臂识别问题的极小极大样本复杂度理论。研究发现，虽然在某些特定行动集下自适应策略仅能带来对数级的改进，但存在某些行动集结构使得自适应策略相对于非自适应策略能实现多项式级别的样本复杂度优势。此外，本文提出了一种高效的$\ell_2$范数估计子程序作为实现这一改进的关键。

Abstract: We study the minimax sample complexity of $\varepsilon$-best arm identification in linear bandits. Given a compact action set $\mathcal{X}$ that spans $\mathbb{R}^d$ and an unknown reward vector $θ\in\mathbb{R}^d$, the goal is to output an arm $\widehat{x}\in\mathcal{X}$ such that $\langle \widehat{x},θ\rangle \ge \max_{x\in\mathcal{X}} \langle x,θ\rangle - \varepsilon$ with probability at least $1-δ$, using as few samples as possible.
  First, we present a non-adaptive fixed-design method with sample complexity $\mathcal{O}\!\left(\frac{d\log(1/δ)}{\varepsilon^2}+\frac{w(\mathcal{X})^2}{\varepsilon^2}\right)$, where $w(\mathcal{X})$ is a Gaussian width term dependent on $\mathcal{X}$, and we prove a matching lower bound $Ω\!\left(\frac{d\log(1/δ)}{\varepsilon^2}+\frac{w(\mathcal{X})^2}{\varepsilon^2}\right)$ for all non-adaptive fixed-design methods.
  We then turn to adaptive sampling. We raise an important structural question: beyond the canonical basis, are there structured action sets for which adaptivity yields only logarithmic-factor improvements over the optimal non-adaptive rate? We answer in the affirmative for several natural action sets, namely the hypercube, the $\ell_2$ ball, $m$-sets, and multi-task multi-armed bandits.
  Finally, we provide the first construction of an action set $\mathcal{X}$ for which adaptivity yields a polynomial-factor improvement over every non-adaptive algorithm. A key ingredient behind this separation is an $\ell_2$-norm estimation subroutine: we design an adaptive algorithm that uses $\mathcal{O}\!\left(\frac{d\log(1/δ)}{\varepsilon^2}\right)$ samples from the unit $\ell_2$ ball in $\mathbb{R}^d$ and outputs an estimate $\widehat r$ satisfying $|\widehat r-\|θ\|_2|\le \varepsilon$ with probability at least $1-δ$, where $θ$ is the unknown reward vector.

Abstract: Manufacturable chip layouts must satisfy thousands of geometry-based design rules, and design rule checking (DRC) enforces them by running executable DRC scripts on layouts. Translating natural language rules into correct DRC scripts is labor-intensive and requires specialized expertise, motivating LLM agents for DRC script synthesis and debugging. However, existing benchmarks have small evaluation sets and often evaluate scripts by code similarity rather than execution correctness, and prior machine learning-based methods either ignore execution feedback or require labeled test layouts as agent's input. To this end, we introduce Rule2DRC, a large-scale benchmark for DRC script coding agents with 1,000 rule-to-script tasks and 13,921 evaluation chip layouts for execution-based scoring. Rule2DRC provides an evaluation pipeline that measures functional correctness via DRC execution outcomes without requiring evaluation layouts as input to the agent. We also propose SplitTester, a tester agent for program selection that uses execution feedback to generate discriminative test cases and separate previously indistinguishable candidate scripts, substantially improving Best-of-N selection performance in this domain. ### [125] [Interaction-Aware Influence Functions for Group Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15675)
*Jaeseung Heo,Kyeongheung Yun,Youngbin Choi,Sehyun Hwang,Jungseul Ok,Dongwoo Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种交互感知影响函数，通过对目标函数在训练参数附近进行二阶泰勒展开，在传统的一阶影响函数基础上增加了一个成对交互项。该交互项显式地量化了两个样本对目标函数影响的对齐程度，从而能够刻画数据之间的冗余或互补关系。

Result: 在六组数据集-模型组合的实验中，新方法在跟踪“留组重训（leave-group-out retraining）”方面的表现远优于一阶影响函数。此外，在Llama-3.1-8B指令微调的数据选择任务中，该方法在七项下游任务中的五项表现超过了基线方法，解决了标准影响函数在某些情况下甚至不如随机选择的问题。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的交互感知影响函数成功地建模了训练数据之间的联合影响，弥补了传统一阶影响函数无法捕捉数据间冗余或互补关系的缺陷。实验证明，该方法在评估数据组影响及指导指令微调任务中均表现出显著优于传统基线方法的性能，为模型的可解释性和高效数据选择提供了新工具。

Abstract: Influence functions approximate how removing a training example changes a quantity of interest, called the target function, such as a held-out loss. To estimate the influence of a group of examples, the standard practice is to sum the individual influences of its members. However, this sum does not capture how examples jointly affect the target: a pair of examples may be redundant or complementary, but the sum cannot distinguish these cases. We propose an interaction-aware influence function that characterizes how interactions between examples influence the target. By expanding the target to second order around the trained parameters, we obtain an estimator that augments the standard sum with a pairwise interaction term that captures the alignment between two examples' effects on the target. We empirically evaluate our estimator in two settings. First, on six dataset-model pairs spanning logistic regression, MLPs, and ResNet-9, our estimator tracks leave-group-out retraining substantially better than first-order influence across all settings. Second, when used as a greedy selection rule for instruction-tuning data on Llama-3.1-8B, it beats prior influence-based and representation-similarity baselines on five of seven downstream tasks, in a regime where standard influence-based selection underperforms random selection.

*Qingyuan Yang,Dongyue Chen,Da Teng,Junhua Xiao,Jiaji Pan,Shizhuo Deng*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 引入交叉分支门控（Cross-branch Gates）：促进实部和虚部频率流之间的紧密上下文交互。 2. 设计 Adaptive PhaseGate 机制：提取周期性位置上下文并生成符号修正信号。 3. 应用自适应信任机制（Adaptive Trust Mechanism）：在样本、变量和通道级别动态控制修正强度，确保周期信息的有效性和模型效率。

Abstract: Long-term time series forecasting is essential for decision making in energy, finance, transportation, and healthcare systems. Recent lightweight forecasting models improve efficiency by operating in transformed or linearized spaces, but two challenges remain in frequency-space forecasting. The real and imaginary streams of complex spectra contain complementary information that is often weakly exchanged, and periodic-position cues can help recurring patterns only when they are reliable for the current dataset and prediction horizon. To address these challenges, we propose FRWKV+, an enhanced FRWKV forecasting model for selective periodic-position branch interaction. FRWKV+ first introduces cross-branch gates that exchange compact contexts between the real and imaginary frequency streams, allowing each stream to modulate the other. It then uses the Adaptive PhaseGate mechanism to extract periodic-position context and generate signed corrections to these gates. An adaptive trust mechanism controls the correction strength at the sample, variable, and channel levels, so periodic-position information is admitted as a reliable correction signal while preserving the efficiency of the FRWKV backbone. External benchmark tables report a separately labeled FRWKV-family selected system for manuscript-level comparison, while mechanism-level claims are based on strict matched-seed FRWKV-family ablations and representative component-level ablations. Under this matched protocol, FRWKV+ achieves the largest MSE winner coverage among the family variants and provides clear gains in selected periodic regimes. Component analysis further supports the usefulness of periodic-position context, signed correction, and adaptive trust in these regimes, while revealing boundary cases where simpler correction rules remain preferable.

### [127] [SEED: Targeted Data Selection by Weighted Independent Set](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15691)
*Yuan Zhang,Lifeng Guo,Junwen Pan,Chang Liu,Wenzhao Zheng,Kuan Cheng,Kurt Keutzer,Shanghang Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SEED 是一种新型数据选择管道，通过图论框架结合节点价值校准和局部尺度归一化，从大规模数据中挑选出高质量且多样化的子集，显著提升了多任务模型的训练效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模训练语料库中，如何平衡样本质量与多样性是提高训练效率的关键。现有数据选择方法在处理梯度噪声和异构领域分布时存在局限，导致无法准确衡量样本重要性或在数据分布稀疏区域产生偏差。

Method: SEED 将数据选择建模为相似性图上的加权独立集（WIS）问题，包含两个核心改进：1. 节点价值校准（Node Value Calibration）：通过限制影响估计到双侧显著子空间，滤除梯度噪声；2. 局部尺度归一化（Local Scale Normalization）：根据局部邻域密度自适应调整边阈值，缓解由跨领域分布偏移带来的图结构不平衡。

Result: SEED 方法在指令微调、视觉指令微调和语义分割等多种任务中均优于现有的先进方法。此外，研究构建了 Honeybee-Remake-SEED-200K 数据集，验证了该方法在多模态领域的高效性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: SEED 提出了一种基于图论的数据选择方法，通过节点价值校准和局部尺度归一化有效解决了大规模数据集中的信息噪声和领域分布不均衡问题。该方法显著提升了模型在指令微调和语义分割等任务上的性能，证明了在有限数据下实现高质量模型训练的可行性。

Abstract: Data selection seeks to identify a compact yet informative subset from large-scale training corpora, balancing sample quality against collection diversity. We formulate this problem as a Weighted Independent Set (WIS) on a similarity graph, where nodes represent data samples weighted by influence, and edges connect semantically redundant pairs. This formulation naturally yields subsets that are simultaneously high-quality and diverse. However, two challenges arise in practice: naive node weights fail to distinguish informative signals from gradient noise, and edge construction under heterogeneous domain distributions produces structurally imbalanced graphs that bias selection toward sparse regions. To address these issues, we introduce two principled refinements from a unified graph perspective: (1) \textit{node value calibration} that restricts influence estimation to the bilateral salient subspace to ground node importance in task-relevant signals rather than surface-level statistics; (2) \textit{local scale normalization} that adapts edge thresholds to local neighborhood density, mitigating graph imbalance induced by cross-domain distribution shifts. Together, these components yield a robust and scalable data selection pipeline dubbed SEED. We further construct \texttt{Honeybee-Remake-SEED-200K}, a compact multimodal dataset curated by SEED. Extensive experiments show that SEED consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods on instruction tuning, visual instruction tuning, and semantic segmentation across diverse model families.

### [128] [Tighter Regret Bounds for Contextual Action-Set Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15692)
*Zijun Chen,Zihan Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种适用于动作集合随情节变化的新型强化学习框架，证明了扩展后的MVP算法在对抗性和随机性环境下均具有最优的遗憾界，并提供了在较大次优间隙下性能更好的界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现实的强化学习应用中，可执行的动作集合往往随环境或任务情节的变化而改变。现有的强化学习算法大多假设动作空间固定，无法直接适应这种动态变化。因此，研究旨在将强化学习框架扩展到具有情节依赖动作约束的情境，并分析算法的性能保证。

Method: 研究将现有的MVP（Minimum Value Policy）算法扩展至具有情节依赖动作约束的框架中。通过理论分析，推导了该算法在对抗性上下文和随机上下文下的极小极大遗憾界（Minimax Regret Bound），并进一步推导了依赖于次优间隙的遗憾界（Gap-dependent Regret Bound）。

Result: 1. 在对抗性上下文中，实现了 $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{SAH^3K\log L})$ 的极小极大遗憾界；2. 在随机上下文中，遗憾界为 $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{SAH^3K})$，样本复杂度为 $\widetilde{O}(SAH^3/ε^2)$；3. 导出了与全局 $p$-修剪正间隙阈值相关的遗憾界，该界在存在显著次优间隙时优于极小极大速率。

Conclusion: MVP算法在处理具有情节依赖动作约束的强化学习问题上具有普适性。研究通过理论证明了该算法在对抗性上下文下达到极小极大遗憾界，并在随机上下文下具备良好的样本复杂度，同时也提供了基于次优间隙的改进遗憾界，证明了其在实际应用中的高效性。

Abstract: We study episodic reinforcement learning with fixed reward and transition functions, but with episode-dependent admissible action sets that are observed at the start of each episode. Performance is measured by cumulative regret against the episode-wise optimal value, $\sum_{k=1}^K [V^{*,M^k} - V^{π^k,M^k}]$, where $M^k$ represents the action context in the $k$-th episode. We show that the MVP algorithm naturally extends to this framework and enjoys strong theoretical guarantees. In particular, we establish a minimax regret bound of $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{SAH^3K\log L})$ for adversarial contexts, where $L$ denotes the number of possible contexts. This result implies a regret bound of $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{SAH^3K})$ for stochastic contexts. We further translate the stochastic regret guarantee into a sample complexity bound of $\widetilde{O}(SAH^3/ε^2)$ for a fixed context distribution.
  In addition, we derive a gap-dependent regret bound of \[ \widetilde O\left( \inf_{p\in [0,1)} \left( \frac{1}{Δ_{\min}^{p}} + pKΔ_{\min}^{p} \right)\log K \cdot \mathrm{poly}(S,A,H) \right), \] where $Δ_{\min}^{p}$ is the global $p$-trimmed positive-gap floor over suboptimal $(h,s,a)$ triples. This bound can substantially improve upon the minimax rate when the relevant suboptimality gaps are large.

### [129] [Going Beyond the Edge: Distributed Inference of Transformer Models on Ultra-Low-Power Wireless Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15694)
*Alexander Gräfe,Ding Huo,Johannes Berger,Marco Zimmerling,Sebastian Trimpe*

TL;DR: CATS 是一个专为超低功耗物联网设备设计的分布式 Transformer 推理框架，通过通信优化的模型并行和鲁棒性训练，使多台协同设备能够运行远超单个设备容量的大型模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种通信感知的分布式推理框架 CATS：1. 开发了“SomeGather”通信原语，通过有选择地广播激活值列来降低带宽和内存需求；2. 基于该原语设计了高效的模型并行划分方法；3. 采用训练阶段的“消息丢失（message-dropout）”策略，增强了模型对无线通信不可靠性的鲁棒性。

Result: 通过在最多 16 台设备上的实机部署实验，CATS 能够实现比单台设备大 14 倍的 Transformer 模型推理，并证明了其在面对无线通信不稳定性时的有效性。

Conclusion: CATS 为超低功耗物联网设备在资源受限的情况下运行大型 Transformer 模型提供了切实可行的分布式推理方案，验证了协同计算在边缘计算领域的可扩展性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Transformer models are rapidly becoming a cornerstone of modern Internet of Things (IoT) applications, yet their computational and memory demands far exceed the capabilities of a single typical ultra-low-power IoT device. We present CATS, a framework for distributed transformer inference on ultra-low-power wireless devices, enabling multiple devices to collaboratively execute models far larger than what a single device can sustain. At its core, CATS is a communication-aware distributed transformer inference scheme co-designed across transformer partitioning, wireless communication and training. It employs SomeGather, a new pruned communication primitive that selectively broadcasts activation columns to reduce communication bandwidth and RAM usage without sacrificing model accuracy. Building on SomeGather, we design a partitioning method that exploits this primitive for efficient model parallelism. To cope with unreliable wireless communication, CATS employs message-dropout during training, which mimics packet losses and yields models that are robust to message loss during inference. In real-world experiments, we show that CATS brings distributed transformer inference to ultra-low-power wireless devices for the first time, with deployments on up to 16 devices that collaboratively execute transformer models up to 14 times larger than what a single device can run.

</details>


### [130] [AGOP-IxG: A Gradient Covariance Filter for Local Feature Attribution on Tabular Data, with a Controlled Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15700)
*Raj Kiran Gupta Katakam*

We propose AGOP-IxG, a fast per-sample attribution method for tabular classifiers that pre-multiplies the per-sample gradient by a top-$K$ rank-truncated Average Gradient Outer Product matrix, and evaluate it against four widely-used baselines on a controlled tabular benchmark designed for AutoML practitioners. AGOP-IxG leads on Spearman rank correlation and noise feature mass on all three synthetic datasets, and on top-$k$ precision on the interaction dataset. Across all settings, AGOP-IxG is approximately $350\times$ to $1{,}650\times$ faster than SHAP. ### [133] [GOMA: Toward Structure-Driven Multimodal Alignment from a Graph Signal Smoothing Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15723)
*Xu Wang,Xunkai Li,Yinlin Zhu,Rong-Hua Li,Guoren Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多模态对齐忽视图结构上下文的问题，GOMA 提出了一种将冻结的多模态嵌入视为图信号进行优化的框架，通过解耦传播路径、模态证据传播和自适应平滑深度，显著提升了检索性能并缓解了过度平滑问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 GOMA（图优化多模态对齐）框架：1. 学习模态感知的传播算子；2. 执行有限步长的耦合平滑（不使用对角跨模态快捷连接）；3. 自适应地提取节点特定的平滑轨迹，以在语义边界崩溃前保留有用的信息。

Result: 在七个 MAG 基准测试中，GOMA 达到了当前最优（SOTA）或并列最优的检索性能，并且相比现有最强图方法表现出显著更高的稳定性。

Conclusion: GOMA 证明了多模态属性图（MAG）的结构信息可以作为冻结多模态嵌入的有效后处理增强手段。该框架在无需微调基础编码器的情况下，通过解耦和精细化的传播机制，显著提升了跨模态检索的性能与稳定性。

Abstract: Multimodal alignment is commonly learned from isolated image-text pairs via CLIP-style dual encoders, leaving the relational context among entities largely unused. Multimodal attributed graphs (MAGs), where nodes carry multimodal attributes and edges encode corpus structure, provide a natural setting for refining frozen vision-language embeddings. This refinement is challenging: visual, textual, and cross-modal relations often induce different neighborhood geometries, while unrestricted graph propagation can quickly over-smooth retrieval representations. Effectively leveraging graph context therefore requires simultaneously breaking modality-specific topological barriers, controlling the smoothing regime, and preserving informative smoothing before semantic boundaries collapse. We propose Graph-Optimized Multimodal Alignment (GOMA), a structure-driven post-alignment framework that views frozen multimodal embeddings as graph signals and addresses these requirements through a unified retrieval-oriented design. GOMA decouples three key design choices: where messages should flow, how multimodal evidence should propagate, and which smoothing depth should be retained. Concretely, it learns modality-aware propagation operators, performs finite-step coupled smoothing without diagonal cross-modal shortcuts, and adaptively reads out node-specific smoothing trajectories to preserve useful smoothing before collapse. All experiments follow a transductive MAG retrieval protocol where the graph serves only as unlabeled context and diagonal self-pair edges are removed. On seven MAG benchmarks, GOMA achieves state-of-the-art or tied state-of-the-art retrieval and remains substantially more stable than the strongest graph competitor, demonstrating that MAG structure can serve as an effective post-encoder for frozen multimodal embeddings.

*Hosna Oyarhoseini,Jimmy Lin,Amir-Hossein Karimi*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的模型评估排行榜（如LMArena）虽然在模型排名中起核心作用，但其排名的鲁棒性尚不明确。研究旨在揭示这些排行榜在面对少量数据变动时的脆弱性，并提供一种审计工具来量化并改善其稳定性。

Method: 提出了一种基于影响函数（Influence-based approximations）的统一扰动框架，通过对匹配数据进行Drop（删除）、Add（添加）、Flip（反转）以及Player Removal（移除模型）四种结构化操作，量化其对排行榜top-k成员资格、Kendall's tau一致性及置信区间不确定性的影响。

Result: 研究发现现代排行榜极易受到扰动影响：仅需不到1%的针对性扰动即可改变排名榜首、降低Kendall's tau值并改变置信区间。此外，该框架还能实现高效的定向操纵（提升或降低特定模型排名），其效率优于现有的基准方法。

Conclusion: 现有的基于Bradley-Terry模型的排行榜系统对数据扰动高度敏感，缺乏足够的鲁棒性。研究提出的基于影响力的审计框架为评估排行榜稳定性提供了有效工具，并强调了开发更稳健的评估协议的必要性。

Abstract: Evaluation leaderboards such as LMArena play a central role in benchmarking large language models by aggregating pairwise human preferences into model rankings, yet the robustness of these rankings remains poorly understood. We present a unified perturbation framework for analyzing Bradley-Terry leaderboards under structured data modifications using influence-based approximations. Our framework studies three match-level perturbations -- Drop, Add, and Flip -- together with player removal, and evaluates their effects on top-k membership, global ranking consistency via Kendall's tau, and confidence-interval-based uncertainty. Across Chatbot Arena and six additional pairwise-comparison datasets, we show that modern leaderboards are non-robust across all three objectives: sub-1% targeted perturbations can change the top-ranked model, degrade Kendall's tau, and alter confidence intervals. Beyond robustness auditing, we show that the same influence scores enable efficient targeted perturbations, promoting or demoting specific models and reducing target-model uncertainty with fewer actions than previous manipulation and active-sampling baselines. By summarizing these effects with normalized dataset-level robustness scores, our framework provides a practical and helpful tool for auditing leaderboard stability and motivating more robust evaluation protocols.

*Pascal Janetzky,Tobias Schlagenhauf,Stefan Feuerriegel*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有持续学习方法多关注领域内性能，容易导致模型依赖特定领域的虚假特征（捷径学习），导致在部署到未见领域时泛化能力不足。为此，作者提出通过学习领域不变的因果表征来提升模型的泛化与鲁棒性。

Method: 提出了一种结合经验回放（Replay-based）与序列不变性对齐（Sequential Invariance Alignment）的持续学习框架，旨在学习并维持跨领域的不变表征，从而过滤掉特定领域的虚假关联。

Abstract: Continual learning (CL) aims to train models sequentially over multiple domains without forgetting previously learned knowledge. However, existing CL methods optimize for in-domain performance and are therefore prone to learning spurious, domain-specific cues (``shortcut learning''), which limits generalization to unseen domains after deployment. In this paper, we address this limitation through continual learning of domain-invariant representation. We introduce a broad class of CL methods that sequentially learn representations capturing invariant structures across domains. Our methods are motivated by the observation that such invariant structures often preserve the underlying causal mechanisms, which can reduce the risk of overfitting to domain-specific cues and thus offer better out-of-domain generalization. Our proposed CL methods combine replay-based training with a tailored sequential invariance alignment to learn -- and preserve -- invariant structures over time. We evaluate our methods under a deployment-oriented protocol that measures performance on unseen target domains. Across six benchmark and real-world datasets spanning vision, medicine, manufacturing, and ecology, our methods consistently outperform existing CL baselines in terms of generalization to unseen target domains. ### [136] [Practical Validity Conditions for Byzantine-Tolerant Federated Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15887)
*Mélanie Cambus,Darya Melnyk,Tijana Milentijević,Stefan Schmid*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对联邦学习中拜占庭容错聚合问题，提出了一种基于“最小包围球（MEB）”的有效性框架。通过引入c-MEB松弛条件，克服了传统凸有效性在维度和适用性上的局限，为评估和设计拜占庭稳健聚合规则提供了新的理论基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的拜占庭容错联邦学习通常依赖于“凸有效性”（Convex Validity）作为核心保证。然而，凸有效性在现代联邦学习系统中存在局限性，具体表现为：其恢复力受维度依赖影响较大，且无法覆盖许多实际有效的聚合规则。因此，本文旨在寻找一种更加灵活、且适用于主流聚合算法的几何有效性条件，以提升聚合的稳健性。

Method: 本文引入了最小包围球（MEB）有效性条件及其乘法松弛形式（c-MEB）。作者推导了实现该条件的最优MinMax-MEB规则，证明了在超过半数客户端诚实（n>2t）的条件下该规则的可实现性。此外，本文对现有的几种标准聚合器（如最小直径平均、Medoid和几何中位数）进行了MEB有效性分析，并将其与现有的凸有效性、松弛凸有效性和箱型有效性进行了系统性的理论对比。

Result: 研究表明，精确的MEB有效性在恢复力上仍然有限，但松弛的c-MEB有效性（c<√2）在n>2t的条件下是可实现的。作者成功推导出了一种最优的MinMax-MEB规则，并验证了多种主流聚合器满足松弛MEB有效性。这些结果系统地构建了分布式计算中几何有效性条件的完整映射，验证了MEB有效性作为凸有效性实用替代方案的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种全新的“最小包围球（MEB）有效性”条件，特别是其乘法松弛版本（c-MEB），为拜占庭容错联邦学习提供了一个比传统凸包有效性更具实用性和普适性的理论框架。研究通过建立几何有效性条件与现有聚合规则之间的映射，证明了在满足多数诚实节点的条件下，relaxed MEB有效性是实现稳健聚合的理想选择。

Abstract: Robust aggregation is the core operation in Byzantine-tolerant federated learning. To ensure the quality of aggregation independently of data distribution or attacks, validity conditions are needed. They provide geometric guarantees of where the output of the aggregation must lie. The widespread convex validity requires the output to lie in the convex hull of the honest vectors. Although this guarantee is strong in theory, it is poorly suited to modern federated learning systems, as it has dimension-dependent resilience and excludes many practical aggregation rules.
  We introduce the minimum enclosing ball (MEB) validity condition for robust aggregation, as well as its multiplicative relaxation, $c$-MEB validity, where $c$ is a constant. We show that exact MEB validity still suffers from limited resilience, while relaxed $c$-MEB validity is achievable if a majority of clients is honest, i.e. $n>2t$. We give an optimal MinMax-MEB rule for the relaxed condition with the bound $c<\sqrt{2}$ and prove explicit relaxed-MEB guarantees for standard aggregators including minimum-diameter averaging, medoid and geometric median. Finally, we relate MEB validity to convex, relaxed-convex and box validity studied in prior literature, thus providing a systematic map of geometric validity conditions for Byzantine-robust aggregation. Our results show that relaxed MEB validity connects validity conditions in distributed computing and Byzantine-tolerant aggregation rules, and offers a practical alternative to convex validity.

Abstract: Parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) has emerged as an critical technique for adapting large-scale foundation models across natural language processing and computer vision. While existing methods such as low-rank adaptations achieve parameter efficiency via low-rank weight updates, they are limited in their ability to preserve the geometric structure of pretrained representations. Our method maintains low computational complexity while maintaining orthogonality with controlled approximation error. ### [138] [Entropy-Based Characterisation of the Polarised Regime in Latent Variable Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15965)
*Peter Clapham,Lisa Bonheme,Marek Grzes*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于信息论的通用判据，用于识别变分自编码器（VAE）中的潜变量极化现象，并证明了即便被归类为“被动”的维度，若经过适当处理，依然能对下游任务起到正向作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的VAE活跃维度识别准则高度依赖高斯先验假设，限制了其在不同变分模型及先验分布下的通用性。此外，关于“极化机制”（latent variables separation）及其对信息表达的影响仍缺乏统一的分析框架。

Method: 提出了一种基于均值表示熵（entropy of the mean representation）的信息论分类方法，用以量化极化状态；通过熵-方差界限（entropy-variance bounds）从理论上推导了该判据与KL散度最小化之间的耦合关系，并结合方差表示信息对该判据进行了验证与完善。

Result: 实验证明，该熵判据能够一致地识别β-VAE、可识别VAE、最小体积自编码器及L2正则化自编码器中的极化状态；研究还揭示了被动维度在适当归一化下仍具备信息承载潜力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于均值表示熵的信息论判据为识别VAE的极化机制提供了一个通用框架。研究表明，“被动”维度并非完全丧失信息，通过适当的归一化处理，这些维度仍能对下游任务产生积极贡献。

Abstract: Variational Autoencoders (VAEs) often exhibit a polarised regime in which latent variables separate into active, passive, and mixed subsets. Existing criteria for identifying active dimensions depend on a Gaussian prior, limiting their applicability to variational models and specific priors. We propose a simple information-theoretic classification of the polarised regime based on the entropy of the mean representation. We show theoretically how this entropy couples to KL minimisation through entropy--variance bounds, and we relate the resulting criterion to Bonheme's active/passive conditions. We also clarify a key limitation: entropy of the mean alone cannot reliably distinguish active from mixed dimensions without additional signals from the variance representation. Empirically, we evaluate the entropy criterion on $β$-VAEs, identifiable VAEs, Least-Volume Autoencoders, and L2-regularised autoencoders, and find that it consistently recovers a polarised regime when such a regime is present across the model classes studied. Finally, we show that passive dimensions can yield small but consistent improvements on downstream tasks when latent codes are appropriately normalised, suggesting that collapse is often a matter of scale rather than absolute information removal.

Our extensive experiments demonstrate that CT-AGD achieves the same level of accuracy as the baseline first-order methods, yet reduces the required training epochs by 33% on average.

### [140] [Mind Dreamer: Untethering Imagination via Active Latent Intervention on Latent Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16030)
*Shaojun Xu,Xiaoling Zhou,Yihan Lin,Yapeng Meng,Xinglong Ji,Luping Shi,Rong Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Mind Dreamer (MD) 提出了一种基于主动潜在干预的新型 MBRL 框架，通过从学习到的生成器中采样“非连续”初始状态来跨越认知盲区，并利用中继值函数处理这些断裂状态间的信用分配，从而显著提升了在稀疏奖励环境下的探索效率和训练速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于模型强化学习（MBRL）受限于“历史束缚”（Historical Tethering），即想象过程通常从观测到的历史状态出发，导致世界模型对环境流形的发现速度远超策略对稀疏奖励的优化速度，造成学习不对称和探索效率低下。

Method: 1. 提出主动潜在干预（ALI）：通过学习到的生成器采样初始状态（s₀），而非仅依赖历史观测，实现对潜在空间“认知盲区”的访问。
2. 引入中继值函数（RVF）与中继不确定性函数（RUF）：在空间断裂处通过类似贝尔曼方程的原理传播价值与不确定性。
3. 定义全局中继流形预期自由能（R-EFE）：将发现过程转化为优化问题。
4. 引入二次折扣因子（γ²）：解决不连续性带来的信用分配难题，确立认知视界。

Result: Mind Dreamer 在 DeepMind Control Suite 基准测试中实现了平均 1.67 倍的加速，特别是在稀疏奖励任务中，其性能提升高达 8.8 倍，证明了其在解决探索瓶颈和提升采样效率方面的有效性。

Conclusion: Mind Dreamer (MD) 通过引入主动潜在干预（ALI）机制，成功打破了传统 MBRL 依赖历史观测状态的马尔可夫连续性限制。理论证明了在不连续状态间进行不确定性传播时，需要采用二次折扣因子（γ²）以建立有效的认知视界。该方法显著加速了模型对稀疏奖励环境的探索，是提升基于模型强化学习采样效率的一项重要技术突破。

Abstract: Model-Based Reinforcement Learning (MBRL) leverages latent imagination for sample efficiency, yet remains constrained by Historical Tethering: imagination is typically initialized from observed states. This creates a learning asymmetry, where the world model's manifold discovery outpaces the policy's sparse-reward optimization. We propose Mind Dreamer (MD), a framework that operationalizes Active Latent Intervention (ALI) to transcend Markovian continuity. MD reformulates discovery as the minimization of a global Relay Manifold Expected Free Energy (R-EFE); by sampling initial states from a learned generator $s_0 \sim p_{gen}(\cdot)$ rather than the historical buffer, MD utilizes an adversarial generator to synthesize non-continuous latent jumps to epistemic blind spots that are physically plausible yet cognitively challenging. To resolve the credit assignment paradox across these spatial ruptures, we derive the Relay Value Function (RVF) and Relay Uncertainty Function (RUF). These potentials treat synthesized anchors as counterfactual intermediary states, propagating pragmatic and epistemic value through a principled Bellman-style formulation. Notably, we prove that uncertainty propagation across discontinuities necessitates a quadratic discount $γ^2$, establishing a formal epistemic horizon. Theoretically, MD approximates a variance-minimizing importance sampler that expands the manifold's spectral gap, reducing the hitting time to critical bottleneck states. Empirically, MD achieves a 1.67$\times$ average speedup over DreamerV3 on DeepMind Control Suite, reaching 8.8$\times$ in sparse-reward tasks.

We theoretically show that under mild conditions, the latent process can be identified from small temporal blocks of observations. ### [145] [Federated Imputation under Heterogeneous Feature Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16099)
*Imane Hocine,Chaimaa Medjadji,Sylvain Kubler,Gregoire Danoy,Yves Le Traon*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对联邦学习中特征空间异构（特征子集不重叠）导致的数据补全效果差的问题，本文提出了FedHF-Impute框架，通过引入全局特征图进行消息传递，实现了跨客户端的间接知识迁移，显著提升了异构数据场景下的补全精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的联邦学习方法（如FedAvg）多假设所有客户端具有相同的特征空间。然而在真实场景中，特别是处理表格数据时，各客户端往往只拥有部分重叠或完全不同的特征子集。这种特征异构性导致参数平均类方法无法在弱重叠或不重叠的特征组间有效传递信息，限制了联邦数据补全的效果。

Method: 作者提出了FedHF-Impute框架，其核心在于将结构性的特征缺失（部分特征空间未观测到）与常规数据缺失区分开来。该方法利用一个共享的全局特征图（Global Feature Graph），通过消息传递机制（Message Passing）在统计相关的特征之间传播信息，从而实现了即使在本地客户端从未同时观测到某些特征组合的情况下，也能进行间接的跨客户端知识迁移。

Result: 在SECOM和AirQuality数据集的模拟部分重叠特征空间实验中，FedHF-Impute的补全精度（RMSE）相比现有联邦学习基线分别提升了26.9%和8.4%；在PhysioNET数据集上，其表现也与最优基线相当（性能差距仅为0.3%）。

Conclusion: FedHF-Impute通过引入全局特征图和消息传递机制，成功解决了联邦学习中异构特征空间下的数据补全难题。该研究证明了利用特征间的统计相关性可以有效实现跨客户端的知识迁移，即使在特征空间完全不重叠的情况下也能提升模型表现，为联邦环境下的数据预处理提供了新的思路。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) enables collaborative training across decentralized clients, but most methods assume aligned feature schemas, an assumption that rarely holds in tabular settings where clients observe only partially overlapping feature subsets. In these heterogeneous feature spaces, parameter-averaging methods (e.g., FedAvg) transfer little information across weakly overlapping or disjoint feature groups, limiting their effectiveness for federated imputation. To overcome this, we propose \textbf{FedHF-Impute}, a federated imputation framework that separates structural feature unavailability from conventional missingness and uses a shared global feature graph to propagate information across statistically related features through message passing. This enables indirect cross-client knowledge transfer, even when features are never jointly observed locally, while preserving standard federated communication. Under simulated partial schema overlap on the SECOM and AirQuality datasets, FedHF-Impute improves imputation accuracy (RMSE) over FL baselines by 26.9\%, and 8.4\% respectively, while achieving comparable performance on PhysioNET, with only a 0.3\% difference relative to the best baseline.

</details>

### [147] [Attention Dispersion in Dynamic Graph Transformers: Diagnosis and a Transferable Fix](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16112)
*Jinhao Zhang,Kangfei Zhao,Qiuhao Zeng,Long-Kai Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对动态图模型在时间分布变化时性能下降的问题，本文指出注意力发散是根本原因，并提出“差分注意力”机制，通过聚焦关键节点显著提升了模型的稳健性与预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于Transformer的连续时间动态图学习模型在面对时间分布偏移（Temporal Distribution Shift）时性能受限，且模型普遍存在注意力机制发散的问题，无法有效聚焦于关键预测节点。

Method: 1. 诊断机制：通过受控消融实验对比关键节点与随机邻居的预测贡献，识别出注意力发散（Attention Dispersion）问题。
2. 模型改进：提出“差分注意力（Differential Attention）”，通过抑制共性注意力分量、增强差异化信号来优化注意力分配。
3. DiffDyG架构：将差分注意力机制集成至现有CTDG Transformer基线中，构建了新的模型框架。

Result: 1. 在9个基准测试和三种负采样协议下，DiffDyG均达到行业领先（SOTA）水平。
2. 在存在剧烈时间偏移的数据集上，性能提升尤为显著。
3. 注意力分析显示，该方法成功降低了注意力熵，并增强了模型对关键节点特征的聚焦能力。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了注意力发散是导致连续时间动态图（CTDG）Transformer在时间分布偏移下性能下降的核心原因。通过引入差分注意力（Differential Attention）机制，能够有效抑制共性信息并放大关键节点的预测信号，显著提升了模型在动态图任务中的鲁棒性和准确性，确立了新的SOTA性能。

Abstract: Transformer-based architectures have become the dominant paradigm for Continuous-Time Dynamic Graph (CTDG) learning, yet their performance remains limited on temporally shifted datasets. In this work, we identify attention dispersion as a shared failure mode of dynamic graph Transformers under temporal distribution shift. Through controlled ablation contrasting structurally and temporally distinguished historical neighbors against random ones, we show that prediction depends on a class of critical nodes that carry consistently more predictive signal than arbitrary neighbors. However, existing Transformers fail to focus on these nodes even when they are present in the input, as temporal shift weakens attention contrast and produces overly dispersed attention distributions. This diagnosis suggests a simple and transferable fix: replace standard attention with differential attention, which suppresses common-mode attention and amplifies distinctive token-level signals. When added to three representative CTDG Transformer baselines, differential attention consistently improves performance, with gains concentrated on high-shift datasets. Attention-level measurements further confirm the mechanism, showing reduced attention entropy and increased attention mass on critical nodes. Building on these findings, we introduce DiffDyG, a reference implementation combining differential attention with standard input encodings. Across 9 benchmarks and three negative sampling protocols, DiffDyG achieves SOTA performance, with especially large gains on the most shifted datasets.

### [148] [MIND: Decoupling Model-Induced Label Noise via Latent Manifold Disentanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16081)
*Dayong Ren*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对基础模型自动标注带来的系统性结构化标签噪声，研究提出MIND框架，通过潜空间解耦与动态聚类，无需真实标注即可有效识别并修正模型诱导的偏差，在多种复杂数据集上表现优异。

Method: 提出了一种名为“模型诱导噪声解耦”（MIND）的框架。该方法引入“潜在解耦估计器”（LDE），通过潜空间解耦将高维噪声流形拆解为可处理的子空间相关分量，并在无需真实锚点的情况下，通过动态投影将样本聚类至具有一致错误模式的潜在结构簇中，从而实现噪声的可识别性。

Conclusion: MIND框架通过潜在空间解耦有效解决了由预训练模型诱导的系统性标签噪声问题，证明了该方法在处理复杂几何结构噪声及纠正视觉语言模型幻觉方面的有效性，为基础模型的鲁棒蒸馏提供了新范式。

Abstract: The paradigm of learning from automatic annotations driven by pre-trained experts and Foundation Models dominates data-hungry applications. However, it introduces a critical challenge: model-induced label noise. Unlike stochastic noise in classical robust learning, this noise stems from annotator inductive biases, manifesting as systematic errors tightly coupled with local feature manifolds. Existing methods relying on global transition matrices underfit these structural patterns, while learning instance-specific matrices remains mathematically intractable. We propose Model-Induced Noise Decoupling (MIND), a theoretically grounded framework addressing this dilemma. We demonstrate that the high-dimensional noise manifold can be decoupled into tractable, subspace-dependent components via Latent Manifold Disentanglement. Specifically, our Latent Decoupling Estimator (LDE) dynamically projects samples into latent structural clusters with consistent error modes, facilitating noise identifiability without ground-truth anchor points. To rigorously evaluate robustness, we adopt a hierarchical protocol: moving from controlled noise on CIFAR-100 to a structural stress test on large-scale real-world 3D datasets (S3DIS, ScanNet), where error patterns explicitly couple with geometric manifolds. Empirically, MIND significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods on these complex benchmarks and effectively corrects zero-shot hallucinations from Vision-Language Models (e.g., OpenSeg), highlighting its potential as a robust distillation framework for Foundation Models.

Method: 提出了一种基于条件边际熵率的离散化目标函数，旨在分离端点条件桥几何结构与边际流演化。据此推导并构建了一种无需训练的熵推理时间调度器（Entropic Inference-time Scheduler），该方法通过在边界处增加采样密度（U 型分布）来优化采样路径。

Flow matching and Schrödinger bridges define probability paths, yet their inference grids are usually heuristic or inherited from one-endpoint diffusion. We derive a conditional-marginal entropy-rate objective for bridge-aware discretization, separating endpoint-conditioned bridge geometry from marginal flow evolution, and use it to build a training-free entropic inference-time scheduler from first principles. For Gaussian Brownian bridges this rate is closed-form and U-shaped, motivating boundary-heavy nonuniform grids. Abstract: Despite their ubiquity, variational autoencoders (VAEs) inherently suffer from posterior collapse, a failure mode in which latent variables are effectively ignored. This failure arises because explicit prior imposition drives optimization toward loss landscape regions corresponding to uninformative latent representations. Here, we introduce Entropic Autoencoders (EAEs), a framework in which reconstruction loss is the only explicit objective, and entropy generates the latent variables' prior implicitly through a free energy-minimizing ensemble of encoders. We demonstrate that EAEs mitigate posterior collapse by learning non-Gaussian, multimodal latent distributions that yield diverse, data-consistent generations and preserve different forms of underlying structure in the data. ### [151] [BAPR: Bayesian amnesic piecewise-robust reinforcement learning for non-stationary continuous control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16170)
*Yifan Zhang,Liang Zheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对分段平稳环境下的鲁棒RL问题，本文提出了BAPR算法，通过集成贝叶斯变化检测实现性能与鲁棒性的自适应切换，并利用Lean 4完成了全过程的形式化验证，有效解决了传统方法在切换点处的稳定性风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在分段平稳的现实控制系统中，现有的鲁棒强化学习方法存在根本性的两难困境：全局保守策略会在平稳阶段浪费性能，而局部自适应策略在环境发生突变时又容易导致灾难性失效。因此，需要一种能够平衡性能与鲁棒性，并能应对突发环境切换的策略。

Method: 1. 提出了BAPR（贝叶斯遗忘型分段鲁棒SAC）算法：将BOCD与鲁棒集成RL相结合。
2. 定义了基于冻结信念分布的凸组合Bellman算子，并证明其满足γ-收缩性。
3. 利用Lean 4进行形式化验证：通过反例界定了收缩失效的边界，并推导了组件级的形式化误差预算。
4. 设计了自适应保守机制：在检测到变化点后增加保守性，并随置信度提升逐渐放松。
5. 采用上下文条件模块，通过RMDM损失训练，在部署时无需模式标签。

Result: 1. 成功证明了所提BAPR算子满足γ-收缩性，并明确了导致收缩失效的数学条件（γ+λΔ≥1）。
2. 在Lean 4中完成了所有理论结果的机器验证（1,145行代码，22个定理，无漏洞）。
3. 实现了有效的自适应保守机制，其检测延迟为O(log(1/δ))。
4. 验证了该方法能够在不依赖部署阶段模式标签的前提下，实现模式感知的鲁棒控制。

Conclusion: 本文提出的BAPR框架通过结合贝叶斯在线变化检测（BOCD）与鲁棒集成强化学习，有效解决了非平稳环境中鲁棒性与性能之间的权衡问题。该研究通过Lean 4进行了全面的形式化验证，确保了算子的收缩性质及误差边界，为复杂动态环境下的安全决策提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Real-world control systems frequently operate under \emph{piecewise stationary} conditions, where dynamics remain stable for extended periods before undergoing abrupt regime changes. Standard robust RL methods face a fundamental dilemma: a globally conservative policy wastes performance during stable periods, while a locally adaptive policy risks catastrophic failure when the regime changes undetected.
  We propose \textbf{BAPR} (Bayesian Amnesic Piecewise-Robust SAC), which unifies Bayesian Online Change Detection (BOCD) with robust ensemble RL. The BAPR operator -- a convex combination of mode-conditional Bellman operators weighted by a frozen belief distribution -- is a $γ$-contraction. A complementary counterexample, machine-verified in Lean~4, establishes a \emph{sharp boundary}: when beliefs depend on the Q-function, the contraction factor becomes $γ+ λΔ$ (where $Δ$ is the mode reward gap), and contraction fails exactly when $γ+ λΔ\geq 1$. We derive a \emph{component-wise} formal error budget for the abstract operator -- every component machine-verified -- bounding post-switch recovery; the budget applies to the abstract mode-mixture operator and inherits to the implemented shared-critic algorithm only through the frozen-parameter design intuition. All results are formally verified with no \texttt{sorry} (1,145 lines across 3 Lean~4 files, 22 machine-verified theorems). BOCD drives an adaptive conservatism mechanism: the policy becomes maximally conservative after detected change-points and smoothly relaxes as confidence grows, with detection delay $O(\log(1/δ))$. A context-conditioning module trained via RMDM loss provides mode-aware representations from simulator-provided mode IDs at training time and requires no mode labels at deployment.

*Zhuoyuan Li,Aiqing Zhu,Qianxiao Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于广义昂萨格原理的通用动力学学习框架，通过在物理约束空间内学习介观动力学，在保证模型理论适定性和物理一致性的同时，实现了对复杂多尺度系统的准确建模与物理可解释性诊断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统科学建模依赖于针对特定问题的固定有效方程，在处理复杂的多尺度系统时面临巨大挑战。为了解决这一问题，研究者旨在开发一种通用的、具有物理约束的动力学学习框架，以摆脱对特定问题建模的依赖，提高建模的鲁棒性和可解释性。

Method: 1. 构建一个包含耗散和保守动力学的统一数学框架，基于广义昂萨格原理（Generalized Onsager Principle）。
2. 在该框架内定义一个受数学约束的假设类（hypothesis class），确保所有模型成员在学习前即满足全局适定性、渐近稳定性、唯一分解可辨识性和离散能量耗散等理论性质。
3. 利用不同问题实例的数据，在上述假设空间内进行动态模型的识别与学习。
4. 通过连续PDE模型和未知的微观链模型进行实证验证。

Result: 1. 建立了一套严谨的理论保障体系，使得学习出的模型在训练前就具备物理一致性。
2. 实验表明，该方法在连续PDE模型数据和未知微观链模型数据上均能实现准确、稳健的动力学预测。
3. 该方法不仅能有效学习动力学，还能为底层物理机制提供有价值的可解释性诊断。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种基于广义昂萨格原理的介观动力学学习新范式。通过在数学约束的假设空间内进行学习，不仅确保了模型在学习前就具备良好的理论特性（如适定性、稳定性等），还通过数据驱动的方式实现了对复杂系统动力学的准确建模，为科学建模提供了一个既具备物理可解释性又具备鲁棒性的通用框架。

Abstract: Traditional scientific modeling typically begins with fixed, instance-wise effective equations and then carries out equation-specific analysis and computation, a procedure that becomes exceptionally challenging in complex applications such as multiscale systems. We propose an alternative paradigm by learning mesoscopic dynamics within a mathematically constrained hypothesis class. Building upon a generalized Onsager principle, we introduce a unified framework encompassing both dissipative and conservative mesoscopic dynamics. We establish uniform and a priori theoretical guarantees, including global well-posedness, asymptotic stability, unique factorization identifiability, and discrete energy dissipation, applicable to all spatio-temporal evolution equations within this hypothesis class prior to all learning stages. Data from each problem instance is then used to guide the identification of members within our hypothesis class, giving rise to accurate, robust and interpretable dynamical models. We empirically validate this framework on both data from continuum PDE models as a check, and on data arising from microscopic chain models for which exact meso-scale models are unknown. The proposed approach not only acts as an effective dynamics learner, but also offers vital interpretable diagnostics of the underlying physics.

</details>


### [154] [The Privacy Price of Tail-Risk Learning: Effective Tail Sample Size in Differentially Private CVaR Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16219)
*El Mustapha Mansouri*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了差分隐私环境下 CVaR 学习的根本局限：隐私机制导致有效样本量由总样本 n 缩减为尾部样本 nτ，并确定了相应的最小化过剩风险速率，证明了处理尾部数据是隐私化 CVaR 学习的本质难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在差分隐私（DP）框架下，标准的经验风险最小化（ERM）目标函数往往难以直接推广到关注分布尾部特征的 CVaR 学习。传统的样本复杂度分析无法直接反映隐私保护对尾部数据分布的敏感性。因此，研究旨在量化差分隐私如何改变 CVaR 学习的有效样本量，并明确隐私预算与尾部概率 τ 对学习误差的具体影响。

Method: 本文采用了理论推导与归约证明的方法：首先推导出标量估计和有限类学习的完全收敛速率（使用纯 DP 并推广至近似 DP）；其次，利用模块化归约方法证明了凸 Lipschitz 学习中隐私项的缩放规律（1/(εnτ)）；最后，通过下界证明验证了所提速率的紧致性，建立了与私有随机凸优化（PSCO）的关联。

Result: 研究发现，差分隐私下的 CVaR 学习有效样本量从 n 缩减为 nτ。在标量估计中，其收敛速率为 Θ(B min{1,(nτ)^{-1/2}+(εnτ)^{-1}})；对于大小为 M 的有限函数类，速率为 Θ(B min{1,sqrt(log(2M)/(nτ))+log(2M)/(εnτ)})。对于凸 Lipschitz 学习，隐私代价项恒定为 1/(εnτ)，证明了尾部数据记录的私有学习是该问题的核心难点。

Conclusion: 本文通过建立严格的上下界，确立了隐私化条件风险价值（CVaR）学习的根本复杂度。研究表明，在差分隐私约束下，CVaR 学习的本质困难在于对尾部有效样本（即 nτ）的私有统计推断。该结论为理解重尾分布下的隐私学习提供了理论基石，并指出 CVaR 优化在隐私保护下的表现受限于尾部样本量的显著压缩。

Abstract: Differential privacy changes the effective sample size governing CVaR learning. For tail mass $τ$, the privacy-relevant sample size is not $n$, but $nτ$; equivalently, the effective private tail sample size is $εnτ$. Private CVaR excess risk decomposes into ordinary tail-risk statistical error and a privacy price. This decomposition is complete for scalar estimation and finite classes: scalar estimation has rate $Θ(B \min\{1,(nτ)^{-1/2}+(εnτ)^{-1}\})$, and finite classes of size $M$ have rate $Θ(B \min\{1,\sqrt{\log(2M)/(nτ)}+\log(2M)/(εnτ)\})$. These complete rates hold under pure DP, and their lower bounds extend to approximate DP in the stated small-$δ$ regimes. For convex Lipschitz learning, modular upper and lower reductions show that the CVaR-specific privacy term necessarily scales as $1/(εnτ)$, with dimension dependence inherited from private stochastic convex optimization. Together, these results identify ordinary private learning on $Θ(nτ)$ informative tail records as the canonical hard subproblem inside private CVaR learning.

</details>


### [155] [Dynamics-Level Watermarking of Flow Matching Models with Random Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16239)
*Shuchan Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过在流匹配模型的“速度场”中嵌入密钥扰动来实现水印的技术，该方法在保护生成模型的同时，保证了生成图像的质量及极高的安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的生成模型水印方法通常依赖于修改模型权重或后处理生成样本，这些方法往往面临鲁棒性较差或容易被去除的问题。为了解决这些挑战，作者旨在开发一种更深入、更隐蔽且不牺牲生成模型性能的水印嵌入方案。

Method: 本文提出了一种针对流匹配（flow matching）模型的动力学级水印技术。其核心在于将水印直接嵌入模型学习到的速度场（即连续动力学）中。具体而言，通过在训练过程中引入一个与密钥相关的随机扰动，并将该扰动构建为连续信道上的随机编码；在检测阶段，通过对黑盒模型进行查询来恢复出隐藏信息，且该扰动被精心设计，确保不会改变模型的生成分布。

Result: 在MNIST和CIFAR-10数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法实现了可靠的信息恢复，且生成图像的质量未受损。此外，在没有密钥的情况下，提取出的信息解码准确率处于随机猜测水平，验证了该方案的有效性和安全性。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种在生成模型中嵌入水印的新型方法，即通过扰动连续动力学（速度场）来实现隐写，该方法在不影响生成质量的前提下实现了水印的可靠提取，为生成模型的版权保护和来源溯源提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: We introduce a dynamics-level approach to watermarking generative models. Rather than embedding signals into model weights or outputs, we embed the watermark directly into the learned continuous dynamics -- the velocity field of a flow matching model. We formulate this as random coding over a continuous channel: a key-dependent perturbation is added during training, and the message is recovered at detection time from black-box queries. The perturbation is designed to leave the generated distribution unchanged. Experiments on MNIST and CIFAR-10 across different architectures confirm reliable message recovery, preserved generation quality, and chance-level decoding accuracy without the secret key.

</details>
